<UserId.>110635643184041676815< /UserId.><Rate>3</Rate><review>Though my experience at Jane at the Marketplace has been mostly positive, today in celebration of my sister's birthday...I have a few exceptions.
First of all I must say that our server, Catherine did a very good job. She was cheery, and informative. Ditto the dude in charge running the front end.
I have always liked the environment here: big space, cloth napery and good quality glass and cutlery. A mid priced  restaurant with the class to fill the space with touches that make a difference in our overall enjoyment.
There were 4 of us today and we ordered:
Med Pizza
Blackened plank Salmon with french fries and Mango/Citrus coulis
Turkey Cobb with Gorgonzola
Red Onion Rings
Coconut Cake
Last time here i ordered the (i assume) Special Pizza which was a pretty spectacular Prosciutto, Mushrooms on a white, cheese sauce. A very delicious item. (i've attached a photo of this pizza to this review along with the Med pizza)
This Med Pizza was a major disappointment. The crust was lifeless and tasteless and was an odd tan color: as it it were whole wheat which it doesn't seem to be based on the menu description. Something was off with this dough: not leavened enough? Leavened too much?
The Buffalo Mozz was good but there just wasn't enough Olive tapenade to make an impression. Worst of all, the greens were dry when they should have been dressed. Even dressed with just olive oil, salt and pepper. Where was the Balsamic?
My sister very much enjoyed the Salmon and found the Mango/Citrus  sauce a tasty accompaniment to the fish. The Salmon was of excellent quality and grilled as ordered. A very good dish.
The Turkey Cobb was good: all of the accoutrements were prepared very well though the Gorgonzola pieces were ridiculously big. Odd to be sure. Also the Turkey was good: obviously not deli turkey but either bought or cooked in house. The greens were crispy and fresh.
The Firestone Red Onion Rings are once again pretty perfect: light, well seasoned batter but also fried very very well. This item is a prime example of a simple dish elevated to ultra goodness because all of the pieces are handled with care and in a careful, thoughtful manner.
The Coconut Cake arrived with a candle which was unlit and no one from the staff to sing Happy Birthday. Huh? a 200 buck lunch ($50 check average for each of us 4) and no one could spare the time?
Despite that, this cake is as coco-nutty as you can get. The cake itself was tender, fluffy and redolent of coconut . Both the buttercream and filling were delicious. The portion of cake sits in a milk-style sauce jam packed with coconut flavor. No artificial coconut "extracts" in sight or in the taste of this cake!

< Review>
This has been our marina for about a year now. The marina grounds are kept beautiful! The staff are friendly and always willing to lend a hand. There are laundry facilities a small gym and showers. Everything is kept very clean. The marina is gated with key only entry which makes us feel safe. The boaters in the marina are all friendly and considerate of you and your boat. The location is great easy access to stores, restaurants and banks. The slip fees are average cost for  San Diego call for fees because they can change. And depend on your boat size. We love it!!!<//Review>

<Text>Came across this place a little late in the evening since most other restaurants were closed. Don Perico is in a nice location downtown. Good decor with optional outside seating. A little lax on the cleaning under our table, but the restaurant overall appeared clean. Ordered shrimp ceviche to start: would not recommend. It tasted like the shrimp was pre-cooked and then mixed into some pico with lime and avocado, as opposed to being marinated in a lime juice as a true ceviche should be. Could definitely taste the difference. I ate Enchiladas California and my husband had a Wet Steak Burrito. Not bad at all. 3 stars for the ceviche and our service. We were forgotten about for around 15 min after being seated; the gentleman who brought out the chips and salsa came and checked on twice before our waiter even came by,  then he took our drink orders AFTER we finally ordered food?!?! And no, the restaurant was not busy.  We don't have to return here.</Text></record>

< review>
Really loved this place. The food was fresh and delicious. The service was not only friendly and efficient, but accomodating. They made me a drink that was not on the menu, and also made a take-out item for us that was not on the menu. We had dinner on the patio. The ambience and decor were so nice. The music was perfect...loud enough to hear and to make you relax and get into that South-of-the-Border mood, where your feet can't help but dance a little...ebut not so loud that you couldn't carry on a conversation comfortably. Overall, a perfect way to spend a Napa evening! We will be back!</review>

<text>It was my very first time going here and I had the steak fajitas. but before we had fajitas I ordered the spicy bean dip and the chicken flautas. I'm not a fatty so I didn't eat all of it myself I was there with my fiance.Just want to clear that up before going on with my review. Bean dip was great because they added jalapenos and chorizo in their bean dip which was a nice change of pace because it gave it a little hardness to it and some chick. The chicken flautas were pretty good but not really they were basically deep fried taquitos and I really love flautas and I just was not a fan there was nothing to it they were they don't have very much taste at all. But then when we got to the fajitas that was bad boys were amazing. The steak Was Juicy the vegetables were crisp and fresh and the old sizzling pan was always fun growing up seeing and hearing and it just brings back memories. Overall, it was a great experience and the food was above average definitely but not the flautas. I wouldn't get those again but I would definitely order the bean dip and the fajitas again even though I won't because I'm going to try other things. I would definitely recommend this place to anyone that's in Napa for some good Mexican food and I really chill atmosphere. drinks wise I just had a Coke and some sparkling didn't try any beer or the margaritas next time I probably will and I didn't have any dessert but I don't think I would have dessert there just because there's Ben & Jerry's around the corner and some other good places in Napa. I hope this is helpful to anyone looking for good Mexican restaurants in Napa.</text>< pics>

<rate>5</rate>< text>
Umm HELLO .. who isn't a local and doesn't like Don Perico's?  Been patroning this restaurant since before the earthquake.  When they had that beautiful mural and decor [I LOVE the chairs] in their old location.  new location is roomy, airy and well worth the wait.  This is our go to .. with the kids.  They love it here. We love it here.  With this visit, it was just me and the hubs.  Tried something different this time .. Taquitos .. almost like the flautas, except with corn tortillas instead of flour [duh, I know right?!?!].  Server is always super amazing, had him a couple different times.  Had a margarita here for the first time too.  It was a strawberry one.  Pretty darn good, considering I usually go for a Long Island or an Adios. <3<//text>
